\doxysubsection{Descripción detallada}
! 

! abstract "{}\+Usage Documentation"{} \href{../concepts/json_schema.md\#customizing-the-json-schema-generation-process}{\texttt{Customizing the JSON Schema Generation Process}}

A class for generating JSON schemas.

This class generates JSON schemas based on configured parameters. The default schema dialect is \href{https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema}{\texttt{https\+://json-\/schema.\+org/draft/2020-\/12/schema}}. The class uses {\ttfamily \doxylink{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_aec2a3cb947f9e0fa2aaab106625b3586}{by\+\_\+alias}} to configure how fields with multiple names are handled and {\ttfamily \doxylink{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_a4c1b2ca8ca29a70a201da455f6a70d0d}{ref\+\_\+template}} to format reference names.

Attributes\+: schema\+\_\+dialect\+: The JSON schema dialect used to generate the schema. See \href{https://json-schema.org/understanding-json-schema/reference/schema.html\#id4}{\texttt{Declaring a Dialect}} in the JSON Schema documentation for more information about dialects. ignored\+\_\+warning\+\_\+kinds\+: Warnings to ignore when generating the schema. {\ttfamily self.\+render\+\_\+warning\+\_\+message} will do nothing if its argument {\ttfamily kind} is in {\ttfamily \doxylink{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_af96f3cd5e8cf4b4d246682773ae68dc4}{ignored\+\_\+warning\+\_\+kinds}}; this value can be modified on subclasses to easily control which warnings are emitted. by\+\_\+alias\+: Whether to use field aliases when generating the schema. ref\+\_\+template\+: The format string used when generating reference names. core\+\_\+to\+\_\+json\+\_\+refs\+: A mapping of core refs to JSON refs. core\+\_\+to\+\_\+defs\+\_\+refs\+: A mapping of core refs to definition refs. defs\+\_\+to\+\_\+core\+\_\+refs\+: A mapping of definition refs to core refs. json\+\_\+to\+\_\+defs\+\_\+refs\+: A mapping of JSON refs to definition refs. definitions\+: Definitions in the schema.

Args\+: by\+\_\+alias\+: Whether to use field aliases in the generated schemas. ref\+\_\+template\+: The format string to use when generating reference names. union\+\_\+format\+: The format to use when combining schemas from unions together. Can be one of\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}- `'any_of'`: Use the [`anyOf`](https://json-schema.org/understanding-json-schema/reference/combining#anyOf)
  keyword to combine schemas (the default).
- `'primitive_type_array'`: Use the [`type`](https://json-schema.org/understanding-json-schema/reference/type)
  keyword as an array of strings, containing each type of the combination. If any of the schemas is not a primitive
  type (`string`, `boolean`, `null`, `integer` or `number`) or contains constraints/metadata, falls back to
  `any_of`.
\end{DoxyVerb}


Raises\+: Json\+Schema\+Error\+: If the instance of the class is inadvertently reused after generating a schema. 

Definición en la línea \mbox{\hyperlink{json__schema_8py_source_l00218}{218}} del archivo \mbox{\hyperlink{json__schema_8py_source}{json\+\_\+schema.\+py}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_a8c796d38380e32ca0840ff955d3d6e8d} 
 None pydantic.\+json\+\_\+schema.\+Generate\+Json\+Schema.\+\_\+update\+\_\+class\+\_\+schema (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_ad39ef4cdecbb1b578c0a400a45a6bb4b}{Json\+Schema\+Value}}}]{json\+\_\+schema}{, }\item[{type\mbox{[}Any\mbox{]}}]{cls}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classpydantic_1_1config_1_1_config_dict}{Config\+Dict}}}]{config}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Update json_schema with the following, extracted from `config` and `cls`:

* title
* description
* additional properties
* json_schema_extra
* deprecated

Done in place, hence there's no return value as the original json_schema is mutated.
No ref resolving is involved here, as that's not appropriate for simple updates.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definición en la línea \mbox{\hyperlink{json__schema_8py_source_l01610}{1610}} del archivo \mbox{\hyperlink{json__schema_8py_source}{json\+\_\+schema.\+py}}.

\Hypertarget{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_a3f5b8771dbeb7d4f860a323336912068}\index{pydantic.json\_schema.GenerateJsonSchema@{pydantic.json\_schema.GenerateJsonSchema}!complex\_schema@{complex\_schema}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{complex\_schema()}{complex\_schema()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_a3f5b8771dbeb7d4f860a323336912068} 
 \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_ad39ef4cdecbb1b578c0a400a45a6bb4b}{Json\+Schema\+Value}} pydantic.\+json\+\_\+schema.\+Generate\+Json\+Schema.\+complex\+\_\+schema (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classpydantic__core_1_1core__schema_1_1_complex_schema}{core\+\_\+schema.\+Complex\+Schema}}}]{schema}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Generates a JSON schema that matches a complex number.

JSON has no standard way to represent complex numbers. Complex number is not a numeric
type. Here we represent complex number as strings following the rule defined by Python.
For instance, '1+2j' is an accepted complex string. Details can be found in
[Python's `complex` documentation][complex].

Args:
    schema: The core schema.

Returns:
    The generated JSON schema.
\end{DoxyVerb}

 bool pydantic.\+json\+\_\+schema.\+Generate\+Json\+Schema.\+field\+\_\+is\+\_\+required (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classpydantic__core_1_1core__schema_1_1_model_field}{core\+\_\+schema.\+Model\+Field}} \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} \mbox{\hyperlink{classpydantic__core_1_1core__schema_1_1_dataclass_field}{core\+\_\+schema.\+Dataclass\+Field}} \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} \mbox{\hyperlink{classpydantic__core_1_1core__schema_1_1_typed_dict_field}{core\+\_\+schema.\+Typed\+Dict\+Field}}}]{field}{, }\item[{bool}]{total}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Whether the field should be marked as required in the generated JSON schema.
(Note that this is irrelevant if the field is not present in the JSON schema.).

Args:
    field: The schema for the field itself.
    total: Only applies to `TypedDictField`s.
        Indicates if the `TypedDict` this field belongs to is total, in which case any fields that don't
        explicitly specify `required=False` are required.

Returns:
    `True` if the field should be marked as required in the generated JSON schema, `False` otherwise.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{field\_title\_should\_be\_set()}{field\_title\_should\_be\_set()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_acfafacfc720575456176065b3efc1053} 
 bool pydantic.\+json\+\_\+schema.\+Generate\+Json\+Schema.\+field\+\_\+title\+\_\+should\+\_\+be\+\_\+set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{Core\+Schema\+Or\+Field}]{schema}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Returns true if a field with the given schema should have a title set based on the field name.

Intuitively, we want this to return true for schemas that wouldn't otherwise provide their own title
(e.g., int, float, str), and false for those that would (e.g., BaseModel subclasses).

Args:
    schema: The schema to check.

Returns:
    `True` if the field should have a title set, `False` otherwise.
\end{DoxyVerb}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_a47c365193961ed19fbcaaf6d2dd3ff1e} 
 tuple\mbox{[}dict\mbox{[}tuple\mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_a8ca58791ba8d4a99bae263daba3c4421}{Json\+Schema\+KeyT}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_a44da347d73dda67917af6a234c17ab39}{Json\+Schema\+Mode}}\mbox{]}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_ad39ef4cdecbb1b578c0a400a45a6bb4b}{Json\+Schema\+Value}}\mbox{]}, dict\mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_a16052db0a668d1706188c9b2f50b7f6a}{Defs\+Ref}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_ad39ef4cdecbb1b578c0a400a45a6bb4b}{Json\+Schema\+Value}}\mbox{]}\mbox{]} pydantic.\+json\+\_\+schema.\+Generate\+Json\+Schema.\+generate\+\_\+definitions (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{Sequence\mbox{[}tuple\mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_a8ca58791ba8d4a99bae263daba3c4421}{Json\+Schema\+KeyT}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_a44da347d73dda67917af6a234c17ab39}{Json\+Schema\+Mode}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic__core_1_1core__schema_a1f02ea1f9bd470bc088f9f8ef1dafa84}{core\+\_\+schema.\+Core\+Schema}}\mbox{]}\mbox{]}     }]{inputs}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Generates JSON schema definitions from a list of core schemas, pairing the generated definitions with a
mapping that links the input keys to the definition references.

Args:
    inputs: A sequence of tuples, where:

        - The first element is a JSON schema key type.
        - The second element is the JSON mode: either 'validation' or 'serialization'.
        - The third element is a core schema.

Returns:
    A tuple where:

        - The first element is a dictionary whose keys are tuples of JSON schema key type and JSON mode, and
            whose values are the JSON schema corresponding to that pair of inputs. (These schemas may have
            JsonRef references to definitions that are defined in the second returned element.)
        - The second element is a dictionary whose keys are definition references for the JSON schemas
            from the first returned element, and whose values are the actual JSON schema definitions.

Raises:
    PydanticUserError: Raised if the JSON schema generator has already been used to generate a JSON schema.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definición en la línea \mbox{\hyperlink{json__schema_8py_source_l00345}{345}} del archivo \mbox{\hyperlink{json__schema_8py_source}{json\+\_\+schema.\+py}}.

        value is available.

\Hypertarget{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_a22cd1ebe30da4b90ee64672f84c9750f}\index{pydantic.json\_schema.GenerateJsonSchema@{pydantic.json\_schema.GenerateJsonSchema}!render\_warning\_message@{render\_warning\_message}}
\index{render\_warning\_message@{render\_warning\_message}!pydantic.json\_schema.GenerateJsonSchema@{pydantic.json\_schema.GenerateJsonSchema}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{render\_warning\_message()}{render\_warning\_message()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_a22cd1ebe30da4b90ee64672f84c9750f} 
 str \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} None pydantic.\+json\+\_\+schema.\+Generate\+Json\+Schema.\+render\+\_\+warning\+\_\+message (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_a4261ad252ff6cb5c43a421b9bbd0123b}{Json\+Schema\+Warning\+Kind}}}]{kind}{, }\item[{str}]{detail}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}This method is responsible for ignoring warnings as desired, and for formatting the warning messages.

You can override the value of `ignored_warning_kinds` in a subclass of GenerateJsonSchema
to modify what warnings are generated. If you want more control, you can override this method;
just return None in situations where you don't want warnings to be emitted.

Args:
    kind: The kind of warning to render. It can be one of the following:

        - 'skipped-choice': A choice field was skipped because it had no valid choices.
        - 'non-serializable-default': A default value was skipped because it was not JSON-serializable.
    detail: A string with additional details about the warning.

Returns:
    The formatted warning message, or `None` if no warning should be emitted.
\end{DoxyVerb}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpydantic_1_1json__schema_1_1_generate_json_schema_ad50c6d2ddf5ba117e0d57a8443a59112} 
 \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_ad39ef4cdecbb1b578c0a400a45a6bb4b}{Json\+Schema\+Value}} pydantic.\+json\+\_\+schema.\+Generate\+Json\+Schema.\+sort (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepydantic_1_1json__schema_ad39ef4cdecbb1b578c0a400a45a6bb4b}{Json\+Schema\+Value}}}]{value}{, }\item[{str \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} None }]{parent\+\_\+key}{ = {\ttfamily None}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Override this method to customize the sorting of the JSON schema (e.g., don't sort at all, sort all keys unconditionally, etc.)

By default, alphabetically sort the keys in the JSON schema, skipping the 'properties' and 'default' keys to preserve field definition order.
This sort is recursive, so it will sort all nested dictionaries as well.
\end{DoxyVerb}
